Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageWellTower partner Clover Group senior apartments contact form
URLhttps://clovergroupinc.com/contact/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score902
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 902, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 49. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

solos: Score 32. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 225

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r57, score 212 (Perceivable text content is not included in any landmark)
  • Package axe, test region, score 14 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 14 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 125

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 96 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 28 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 40 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 118

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 61 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 44 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 4 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)
  • Package ibm, test IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA, score 48 (Contrast ratio of text with background does not meet WCAG 2.1 AA)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 42 (Very low contrast)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 66

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r83, score 28 (Overflow is hidden or clipped if the text is enlarged)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 53 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 25

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 18 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 12 (Text has insufficient contrast)

Issue errorReferenceBad

WCAG: 3.3.1

Score: 19

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R41, score 17 (Error message describes no invalid form field value)

Issue iframeTitleBad

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 16

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r13, score 4 (iframe has no accessible name)
  • Package axe, test frame-title, score 3 (Frame has no accessible name)
  • Package continuum, test 228, score 4 (iframe has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.2_4_1.H64.1, score 8 (iframe element has no non-empty title attribute)
  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_Frame_HasTitle, score 4 (Inline frame has an empty or nonunique title attribute)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 14

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 12 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Score: 11
